\subsection*{General information}
Points on lines:
$$
9^{82}$$
Lines on points:
$$
18,\,9^{72},\,1^{72}$$
\subsubsection*{Singular Points}
The surface has 1 singular points:\\
\begin{align*}
S_{0} &= P_{3}=\bP(0, 0, 0, 1) = \bP(0, 0, 0, 1)\\
\end{align*}
